See the article "Webs of rational curves on real surfaces" for an explanation.

The classification table below is generated with the "ns_lattice" Python library and is available on GitHub.com. 


Short description of the column headers
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
rownr  : row number

rank   : rank of Neron-Severi lattice of a real weak del Pezzo surface X (degree equals 10-rank)

Mtype  : Dynkin type of A(X), where A(X) consists of divisor classes that are associated to the involution M acting on the Neron-Severi lattice.

type   : Dynkin type of B(X) which consist of indecomposable (-2)-classes. The components enclosed with {.} are pointwise preserved by M. The components encloded with [.] are not pointwise preverved but preserved as a whole by M.

#-2    : |B(X)|

#-1    : |E_*(X)| where E_*(X) consists of the (-1)-classes that have positive intersection product with classes in B(X)

#fam   : |F_*(X)| where F(X) consists of divisor classes c such that c*c=0, -k*c=2 where k is the canonical class and b*c>=0 for all b in B(X).

#-2R   : same as #-2 column, but with the additional property that the classes under consideration are preserved by the involution M.

#-1R   : |E_R(X)|: same as #-1 column, but with the additional property that the classes under consideration are preserved by the involution M.

#famR  : |F_R(X)|: same as #fam column, but with the additional property that the classes under consideration are preserved by the involution M.

Md_lst : A(X)

d_lst  : B(X)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------



Numbers of rows for each listed rank 
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------- 
rank = 3 : rows = 3 
rank = 4 : rows = 12 
rank = 5 : rows = 12 
rank = 6 : rows = 52 
rank = 7 : rows = 56 
rank = 8 : rows = 252 
rank = 9 : rows = 438 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
